    <div class=" clearFloats bigBox" id="aboutAuthor"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/4432.Jasper_Fforde">About Jasper Fforde</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
      <a href="/author/show/4432.Jasper_Fforde"><img alt="4432" src="http://d.gr-assets.com/authors/1350497674p2/4432.jpg" class="right" /></a>
    <div class="readable">
      
<span id="freeTextContainer9524198853681453629">Jasper Fforde is a novelist living in Wales. He is the son of John Standish Fforde, the 24th Chief Cashier for the Bank of England, whose signature used to appear on sterling banknotes, and is cousin of <a title="Desmond Fforde" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4200171.Desmond_Fforde">Desmond Fforde</a>, married to author <a title="Katie Fforde" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/86097.Katie_Fforde">Katie Fforde</a>. His early career was spent as a focus puller in the film industry, where he worked on a number of films including Quills, GoldenEye, and Entrapment.<br /><br />H</span>
  <span style="display:none" id="freeText9524198853681453629">Jasper Fforde is a novelist living in Wales. He is the son of John Standish Fforde, the 24th Chief Cashier for the Bank of England, whose signature used to appear on sterling banknotes, and is cousin of <a title="Desmond Fforde" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4200171.Desmond_Fforde">Desmond Fforde</a>, married to author <a title="Katie Fforde" href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/86097.Katie_Fforde">Katie Fforde</a>. His early career was spent as a focus puller in the film industry, where he worked on a number of films including Quills, GoldenEye, and Entrapment.<br /><br />His published books include a series of novels starring Thursday Next: <a title="The Eyre Affair" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27003.The_Eyre_Affair">The Eyre Affair</a> (2001), <a title="Lost in a Good Book" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27000.Lost_in_a_Good_Book">Lost in a Good Book</a> (2002), <a title="The Well of Lost Plots" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27001.The_Well_of_Lost_Plots">The Well of Lost Plots</a> (2003), <a title="Something Rotten" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/26999.Something_Rotten">Something Rotten</a> (2004) and <a title="First Among Sequels" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/27002.First_Among_Sequels">First Among Sequels</a> (2007). <a title="The Big Over Easy" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6628.The_Big_Over_Easy">The Big Over Easy</a> (2005), which shares a similar setting with the Next novels, is a reworking of his first written novel, which initially failed to find a publisher. It had the working title of Nursery Crime, which is the title now used to refer to this series of books. The follow-up to The Big Over Easy, <a title="The Fourth Bear" href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/148809.The_Fourth_Bear">The Fourth Bear</a> was published in July 2006 and focuses on Goldilocks and the Three Bears.<br /><br /><strong>Series:</strong><br />* <a href="http://www.goodreads.com/series/43680-thursday-next">Thursday Next</a><br />* <a href="http://www.goodreads.com/series/43679-nursery-crime">Nursery Crime</a><br />* <a href="http://www.goodreads.com/series/51553-shades-of-grey">Shades of Grey</a></span>
  <a onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;" href="#" data-text-id="9524198853681453629">...more</a>

    </div>

Sherlock Holmes is killed at the Reichenbach Falls and his series is stopped in its tracks. And before this can be corrected, Miss Marple dies suddenly in a car accident, bringing her series to a close as well. When Thursday receives a death threat clearly intended for her written self, she realizes what\'s going on: there is a serial killer on the loose in the Bookworld. And that\'s not all--The Goliath Corporation is trying to deregulate book travel. Naturally, Thursday must travel to the outer limits of acceptable narrative possibilities to triumph against increasing odds.           $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});
        } else {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: 6000})});
        }
      });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_13617248').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('bookCover_13617248').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_13617248').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]&gt;
</script>
</li>
</ul>
